Current Affairs Commentary

The Results of the British General Election Announced 14

— Ang

The results of the British general election have been announced. The number of seats won by each party is not outside the expectations of the general public. The National Government holds approximately two hundred and fifty more seats in the House of Commons. Observers say that such an advantage has only been seen since the Great Reform Act of 1831. More than seventy percent of the electorate exercised their right to vote, which is clear evidence of the British people's special concern for national affairs during this tumultuous time in the world. Prime Minister Baldwin, on the evening when the election situation was determined, announced to his countrymen his two great aspirations: to work diligently for national revival and world peace. Party leaders Attlee and Morrison have also expressed their disappointment with the election results. Thus, in the next five years, the guiding spirit of British domestic and foreign policy will continue to be Neo-Conservatism.

This election, on the surface, was a struggle between maintaining the National Government and restoring a party cabinet, but in reality, it was merely a struggle between the two major forces of the Conservative Party and the Labour Party. Baldwin, with his personal prestige, took advantage of the international situation and suddenly announced an early re-election. One purpose was to use diplomacy to consolidate political power, and the other was to enhance the power to curb the East African war through the renewed support of the people. The close interaction between domestic and foreign policy is the principle of modern politics.

However, as far as the Labour Party is concerned, it has already fallen into a difficult situation in this session. Its leaders in the House of Commons, Lansbury, and in the House of Lords, Clifford, resigned due to their opposition to sanctions. The internal divisions within the Labour Party have not yet been repaired. It is quite difficult to find a person in the party to serve as Prime Minister. This is a major weakness in the Labour Party's strategy. Moreover, the economic situation in Britain today is the wealthiest in Europe, and the difference compared to the poverty of 1931 cannot be measured. The Labour Party's failure to gain momentum this time is also due to the circumstances.

However, in this general election, the Labour Party knew early on that it was powerless to seize power. However, there was still something to compete for, namely, the issue of the principle of "correction and balance" in the democratic system, given that the ruling party maintained its overwhelming majority in the House of Commons. This provided an excuse for the opposition party to appeal to the hearts of the British people who love democracy. Therefore, during the election campaign, Lloyd George once said, "If we see an inflated majority again, the danger will be extreme." Snowden also said, "If the election results give the government an uncontrollable majority, it will not only be a great disaster for the country, but also a disaster for the world." Looking at the election results now, the Conservative Party has dropped from 471 seats to 383 seats, and the Labour Party has also increased from 52 seats to 154 seats. It can be seen that the opposition party cannot be said to have been an absolute failure.

Overall, if we look at the overall situation, in terms of region, large cities and rural areas are mostly the domain of the Conservative Party, and most industrial areas belong to the Labour Party. However, there are also those who lean towards the Conservative Party because the protectionist tariffs and the expansion of military demand are beneficial to domestic industry and commerce. The Labour Party failed to "recover lost ground" in Wales, Scotland, and the northern industrial areas in this session, which is a great disappointment. Furthermore, in terms of personnel, MacDonald's defeat is the same fate as Lloyd George's in 1931. It can be said that another political giant has "ended." The leader of the Anti-Government Liberal Party, Samuel, completely failed in this session. Although Simon, the leader of the Liberal Party affiliated with the government, was still elected, the number of votes he received plummeted. From this, it can be seen that liberalism is increasingly declining in Britain. On the other hand, Morrison, who is known as the "strength of the Labour Party," was defeated in 1931 and has now re-entered Parliament. This can be seen as a sign of the Labour Party's resurgence, and it is becoming increasingly clear that the British political stage will maintain a two-party system. As for the reorganization of the cabinet, it is an inevitable trend. It is rumored that the ardent navalist Winston Churchill is slated to succeed as First Lord of the Admiralty, and Eden, who has recently emerged in the international diplomatic arena, will be transferred to Minister of War or Colonial Secretary. Thus, strengthening national defense and uniting the colonies will be the basic tone of British politics in the future.

President of South Manchuria Railway, Matsuoka, Returns to Japan on a Mission 15

(Changchun) After important discussions with the Commander of the Kwantung Army regarding issues in North China and matters to be coordinated with the central government, Matsuoka, President of the South Manchuria Railway, departed by plane from here at 8:00 a.m. today, via North Korea, for Tokyo. He will also need to inspect Chongjin and Gyeongseong en route, so he is expected to arrive in Tokyo around the 23rd. (18th, Dentsu Dispatch)

The Midnight Bell Tolls in Geneva: The League of Nations Implements Sanctions Against Italy; Collective Pressure to End the War is an Unprecedented Historical Event; Italy Refuses to Yield and Demonstrates Nationwide Resistance; Changing Strategy Against Abyssinia to Adopt New Offensive 16

(Geneva) The midnight bell in Geneva rang loudly, signifying the beginning of the world's most peculiar economic war. Participating in this war on one side are the 52 member states of the League of Nations Sanctions Committee, and on the other side is Italy. This implementation of sanctions by the League of Nations member states is an unprecedented historical event in using collective economic and financial pressure to stop the carnage of war. The tolling of the bells signifies the concerted efforts of the entire world to implement this plan. (18th National Telegram)

(Rome) Various countries' sanctions against Italy have been implemented starting today. Italian people generally regard this day as "the most inglorious and unfair date in world history." National flags are hung throughout the country, and people are holding demonstrations everywhere. In the capital, flags are hung in the windows of all residences and shops. Students are parading in groups, singing patriotic songs to express their resistance to the sanctions. Troops are stationed in front of the embassies of the countries participating in the sanctions, especially the British and French embassies, to prevent incidents. (18th Havas Dispatch)

(Rome) Two million students across the country held a grand demonstration today to protest the League of Nations' economic sanctions. Flags were displayed in every household, and shops were closed all day to show the spirit of national unity in Italy. In Rome, 20,000 students marched in front of the embassies of the countries participating in the sanctions, with especially blatant demonstrations in front of the British embassy. The various marching groups are scheduled to gather in front of the Palazzo Venezia at 10:00 p.m., at which time Mussolini will be presiding over the Supreme Council to determine major plans. (18th National Telegram)

(Geneva) The member states of the League of Nations are scheduled to implement sanctions against Italy starting tomorrow. In a few hours, Italy will be almost cut off from the rest of the world economically. According to the resolution of the League of Nations General Assembly, (1) member states must not transport weapons, ammunition, or military supplies to Italy, while Abyssinia, as a country recognized as having been invaded, may still purchase armaments to the best of its ability. All member states will comply with this measure. Only Switzerland, following the example of the United States, has simultaneously banned the shipment of armaments to both belligerent countries, Italy and Abyssinia. (2) Financial sanctions will also be implemented simultaneously. Fifty-two member states have pledged not to provide loans to the Italian government, corporations, or individuals in any form, except for charitable causes such as the Red Cross. These countries will not adopt a barter system with Italy. (3) All member states participating in the sanctions will prohibit the import of Italian goods in order to prevent Italy from finding foreign currency. (4) Participating countries will prohibit the export to Italy of many items necessary for war, such as trucks and various types of gases, starting tomorrow morning. As for coal, oil, and iron, they are not subject to the embargo because non-member countries such as the United States and Germany can continue to sell them to Italy. Of the 58 member states of the League of Nations, excluding the two parties involved, Italy and Abyssinia, 52 have accepted the above measures. However, Austria, Hungary, Albania, and Paraguay have refused to comply. As for the non-member United States, it has simultaneously banned the shipment of armaments to both parties involved, and Egypt has replied to the League of Nations that it will participate in the sanctions. (17th Havas Dispatch)

(Rome) Italy's measures to resist sanctions will be implemented after midnight today. The government has strictly ordered customs authorities at all seaports and borders to comply. All goods from countries participating in the sanctions, even those already in transit, will not be allowed to enter Italy. However, in theory, these measures to resist sanctions do not completely block all foreign products. Raw materials and food may still be allowed to enter Italy with special permission from the authorities. Recently, various raw materials and food have been stockpiled in large quantities, enough to last for some time. Also, for certain secondary products produced by foreign countries, they may still enter the country only if the exporting country accepts Italian goods. (17th Havas Dispatch)

(Rome) Since the League of Nations member states implemented sanctions against Italy, the living conditions in Italy have changed drastically. For example, to save electricity, businesses close at 4:30 p.m. The lunch break for employees has been reduced from two hours to half an hour. Public buses are running less frequently due to a shortage of gasoline. Most employees walk to their offices. Most homeowners do not use heating appliances to save coal. Stores have stopped selling foreign foods. The authorities are urging people to buy "domestic products." Many shopkeepers have been accused of raising prices to hoard goods. (18th Reuters Dispatch)

From the Tigray Province Front, regarding the government's appointment of Chief of the General Staff General Badoglio as High Commissioner of East Africa and Commander-in-Chief of the Italian Forces, military figures here explain that Italy will now focus all its efforts on the Abyssinian issue. Various European events, such as the Brenner Pass incident (the border between Italy and Austria) and others, have been relegated to secondary importance. General Badoglio is Italy's foremost general, and his appointment as Commander-in-Chief is tantamount to devoting the nation's full strength to managing East Africa. From now on, the Abyssinian campaign will become a real war, not just a colonial conquest. (17th Havas Agency Dispatch)

Decision to Sanction Italy: Our Country Prepares to Implement; Currently Studying Methods; Our Representative Sends Letter to the League of Nations 17

(Geneva) Hu Shize, director of the Chinese delegation office at the League of Nations, recently sent a letter to League of Nations Secretary-General Avenol, stating that the Chinese government is currently studying methods to implement the resolutions passed by the Sanctions Adjustment Committee. Once the implementation date is determined, the Secretariat will be notified. (18th Havas Dispatch)

(Nanjing) Regarding the response from our government to the recommendations adopted by the League of Nations Adjustment Committee on sanctions against Italy, Article 3 prohibiting the import of Italian goods, Article 4 prohibiting the export of important raw materials to Italy and its territories, and Article 5 regarding mutual assistance measures, our country's permanent representative to the League of Nations delivered the response to the League of Nations Secretariat on the 29th of last month. The contents are as follows: The Chinese government accepts the recommendations adopted by the Adjustment Committee in Articles 3, 4, and 5 and is currently studying methods to implement them. To the extent possible, the government will implement the recommendations in Articles 3 and 4 on the date designated by the committee but must be notified in a timely manner so that these measures can be implemented on a mutually agreed date. (18th Special Dispatch)

Strong British Public Opinion Supports Sanctions Against Aggressor Nations; France's Position Allows for Choice 18

(Paris) The Paris Echo's correspondent in London interviewed various important British figures, including Foreign Secretary Hoare, regarding the sanctions against Italy, which went into effect today. The results of the interviews proved that British public opinion strongly supports the League of Nations' implementation of sanctions. However, the general British public does not believe that the Italian-Abyssinian conflict can be resolved through various extreme methods, such as blockades and military sanctions. But they all hope that the League of Nations can pass a test. The British people are very angry about Italy's aggression. Therefore, even if the British government does not support participating in collective action, it has no choice but to do so due to public opinion. Another important figure said, "The British people are very angry at any provocation...

Britain Asks Italy's Five Neighboring Countries to Submit Certificates of Origin for Imported Goods to Prevent Italian Goods from Entering by Detour 19

(London) Due to the sanctions against Italy to be implemented today, the British government has notified Germany, Hungary, Austria, Switzerland, and Albania that all goods shipped to Britain from today onwards must be accompanied by a certificate of origin. The purpose is to prevent Italian goods from entering Britain by detour. Germany refused to comply. However, while the British authorities continued to discuss the matter with the German government, they ordered customs to require certificates for all German goods entering the country. It is reported that the British government does not believe that Germany's claim that this measure violates the Anglo-German commercial treaty is valid. (18th Reuters Dispatch)

Changing Traditional Policy, the United States Voices Support for the League of Nations; Exceeding the Powers Granted by Neutrality Laws; Freedom of the Seas Partially Abandoned; Impact Will Extend to the Far East 20

(Washington) President Roosevelt's announcement that the United States Navy and Army will no longer protect American merchants trading with the belligerent countries of Italy and Abyssinia is a reversal of the United States' traditional policy of the past 125 years and a major change in the application of American military force. The President's move also exceeds the legal powers granted by the recently passed Neutrality Laws by Congress. The American people now recognize this as a new "coercive policy," and its impact will extend to the Far East in the future. The key points of this policy are as follows: (1) Supporting the League of Nations' sanctions against aggressor nations within the scope of unilateral action; (2) If the British Navy wishes to implement sanctions, the United States guarantees that it will not conflict with it. This is tantamount to tacitly acknowledging the British Navy as the de facto power in the Mediterranean indefinitely; (3) Applying the same policy to other European countries.

American Gasoline Bound for Italy Seized in Los Angeles 21

Los Angeles The cargo ship "Wolegon," loaded with gasoline and intending to sail to Singapore, has been seized by the Sailors' Union of this place. The chairman of the union wired the prime minister, stating that the gasoline loaded on this ship is clearly intended to be transshipped to Italian Somaliland via Singapore. Therefore, the ship has been seized and will be released only after the State Department guarantees the complete protection of the crew. According to a Reuters dispatch from Washington, State Department officials declined to comment on the matter. (17th Reuters Dispatch)

New Italian Commander Departs for East Africa: Future Strategy to Adopt Rapid Advance; Decisive Battle to Begin Next Month 22

(Rome) The new Commander-in-Chief of the Italian forces in East Africa, General Badoglio, is scheduled to depart for Massawa today. (18th Reuters Dispatch)

Asmara Sources believe that the new High Commissioner of East Africa and Commander-in-Chief of the Italian forces, General Badoglio, will soon change the strategy of the Italian forces on the northern front. The purpose is to proceed expeditiously, using light troops for rapid assaults, relying on new camel transport, supplemented by a systematic air force. The previous approach of advancing while constructing roads is no longer used. The slow advance was suitable but damaging to Italy's reputation. Currently, roads are being built behind the lines directly to the front lines. The policy of road construction before military advancement may be abandoned. (18th Reuters Dispatch)

Tigray Province Front Our Agency's military correspondent, Baer, reports that the newly appointed High Commissioner of East Africa and Commander-in-Chief of the Italian forces, General Badoglio, will depart from Naples around November 19 and arrive at the port of Massawa in East Africa on November 26 or 27. The former High Commissioner, General de Bono, will greet him at the port of Massawa. After General Badoglio arrives at the port, he will return to his country on the original ship. It is generally speculated that the war in the front will be temporarily calm before the arrival of the new commander. Judging from the speed of concentration of Abyssinian troops, the main battle on both sides will likely occur at the end of December. Currently, the Italian Second Army has repelled the Abyssinian troops defending along the Tekeze River. The clearing work in the Gheralta area is proceeding very rapidly, which proves that the number of Abyssinian troops from Aksum to Macalle is very small. In addition, all the aircraft of the Second Army are concentrated on the road from Aksum to Adwa to bomb the Abyssinian defense line attacking the Italian right flank. Also, the Italian army seized communications between Abyssinian General Seyoum and the Abyssinian Emperor in Aksum, proving that the Abyssinian army had to abandon Aksum because it could not stop the advance of Italian tanks. (18th Havas Dispatch)

Tigray Province Front Military experts also believe that after General Badoglio arrives here, Italian military actions will be urged to progress rapidly. The Italian army will complete the connection between the Eritrean and Somaliland armies before the start of the next rainy season. Therefore, future marches will strive for speed. However, it is very difficult for General Graziani's southern army to capture the city of Harar because the area is in the midst of thousands of mountains and valleys, and it is impossible to encircle it without a large number of new weapons. The Graziani division still lacks this. Therefore, the northern army will focus all its efforts on attacking the city of Dessie. After Dessie is captured, the Eritrean army can be transferred to Somaliland to join forces with Graziani. It is generally believed that General Badoglio's first step after taking office will be to disregard the difficult terrain between Macalle and Dessie and rapidly advance towards the city of Gondar. In the past Libyan war, General Graziani was subordinate to General Badoglio, and the two had a very close relationship. (17th Havas Agency Dispatch)

Harar Our Agency's correspondent, Lavua, reports that, according to Abyssinian military figures, the Italian army on the southern Wollega Province front is still 60 kilometers south of the Daggah Bur area. There has been heavy rain in the area recently, so the Italian army has been unable to advance. Prince Tesemma, the son-in-law of the Abyssinian Emperor, is actively replenishing military supplies in the Dolo area (at the intersection of Italian Somaliland, British Kenya, and the southern border of Abyssinia) to prepare to advance towards Daggah Bur. Thirteen wounded Abyssinian soldiers from the area have recently been transported here for treatment. (18th Havas Dispatch)

Addis Ababa Our Agency's correspondent, Ochina, reports that Abyssinian troops appear and disappear unpredictably on the Tigray Province front, hindering Italian military operations. The Italian rear units are often harassed, which has recently been officially confirmed. According to well-informed sources, Abyssinian General Seyoum has bypassed the Italian right flank and reached the area west of the city of Adwa. However, his exact location is still unknown. General Ayalla's troops are now along the Setit River to support General Seyoum. Rumors that General Ayalla has entered Italian Eritrea have not been confirmed. (18th Havas Dispatch)

Marconi Criticizes the League of Nations 24

(Rome) The annual meeting of the Italian Royal Academy opened today. The President of the Academy is Senator Marconi, the famous inventor of radio. In his opening speech, he said, "Starting tomorrow, Geneva will engage in inhumane economic and financial conquests against Italy, which has shared hardships with the majority of countries participating in the sanctions. Now, to repay kindness with malice, who can believe it? What is Italy's crime? The crime is defending the colonial territories conquered at the cost of blood. The crime is spreading culture to dark, primitive tribes. Wherever the Italian flag goes, the light of Christianity is revived, and native tribes offer food and drink to welcome the king's army. But unexpectedly, this is how the League of Nations has been offended." (17th Havas Agency Dispatch)

Eighty-Year-Old Englishman Willing to Serve Italy 25

Egyptian Independence Movement Wishes to Maintain Friendship with Britain but Does Not Want to Become a Dependency; Student Riots Have Not Abated 26

Cairo Nahas, the leader of the Wafd Party and former Prime Minister, told a reporter from the American United Press today that Egypt demands complete independence and a standing army of 10,000 men. The student riots of the past few days have resulted in the deaths of seven people and injuries to more than 200. This is only the prelude to the independence movement. Nahas denied that the movement was being directed by Italy behind the scenes and denied that Egypt was taking advantage of Britain's preoccupation with Italy to pursue its aims. Nahas said, "We want to be friends with Britain, but we do not want to be its dependency. The only demand of the Wafd Party is that Britain fulfill its promises and grant Egypt independence. We do not want to take advantage of others' difficulties, but we are equally opposed to British imperialism and Italian imperialism. Britain knows that the situation is serious, so it is prone to being oversensitive." Regarding British activities in Egypt after the start of the Italian-Abyssinian War, Nahas said, "We oppose the British fleet concentrating in Alexandria without our consent. This is tantamount to being regarded as a colony. We are willing to sign a treaty with Britain allowing the use of our naval ports in wartime, but we must sign the treaty as an independent country." (17th National)

Cairo Hearing that one of the students injured in the riots had died, 800 students rushed to the public hospital today to demand the body of their comrade. Police forcibly prevented the students from entering and fired warning shots into the crowd. Subsequently, British cavalry and local police arrived, rushing back and forth, swinging their sabers to disperse the crowd. The students shouted slogans such as "Down with British imperialism" and "Long live the Wafd Party" and dispersed. (18th National Telegram)

British Cabinet to Be Reorganized; MacDonald and Son Fail in Election; National Cabinet Style to Be Maintained 27

(London) The Baldwin Cabinet has a total of three National Labour Party members: Lord President of the Council MacDonald, his son Colonial Secretary Malcolm, and Secretary of State for War Lord Halifax. MacDonald and his son failed in the election, and Lord Halifax has not yet decided on his position. All three are unlikely to remain in office. However, Prime Minister Baldwin believes that the National Cabinet style should still be maintained and should not be allowed to disintegrate. In addition, other cabinet members such as First Lord of the Admiralty Sir Bolton Eyres Monsell and Secretary of State for Air Sir Philip Cunliffe-Lister did not run for election. Among them, Monsell is likely to abandon political life, and Cunliffe-Lister will be ennobled and enter the House of Lords, remaining a cabinet member. Minister without Portfolio Anthony Eden will likely be transferred to another department. It is still unknown whether the League of Nations Affairs Department will be abolished before the end of the Italian-Abyssinian conflict. Winston Churchill, the leader of the Conservative Party's extremist faction and former Chancellor of the Exchequer, was recently re-elected as a member of Parliament in Epping. Baldwin is likely to invite him to join the cabinet. (18th Havas)

Aftermath of the British Parliamentary Election: Suspicious Circumstances Surrounding the Election of the Minister of Agriculture and Fisheries; Two Recounts Yield Conflicting Results; Labor Party Requests a Re-election 28

(London) During the general election for the Lower House on the 14th of this month, the Minister of Agriculture and Fisheries, Elliot, was elected as a member of the Lower House in the Scottish town of Kilmarnock. The initial vote count showed Elliot winning by only two votes. A second recount showed a majority of 149 votes. The Scottish Labor Party, citing suspicious circumstances in the vote counting, has requested the annulment of the vote and a re-election. (Havas Dispatch, 18th)

Roosevelt Announces the Outline of the US-Canada Trade Agreement: Effective from January Next Year, for a Period of Three Years; Reciprocal Principles to Improve Trade Relations 29

(Washington) President Roosevelt announced tonight that the US-Canada trade agreement, signed at the White House on Friday, will come into effect on January 1st of next year, with a fixed term of three years. After three years, either party can terminate the agreement at any time with six months' notice; otherwise, it will continue indefinitely. According to the provisions of the agreement, Canada will grant special preferential treatment to 767 types of American goods. These preferential measures are divided into four categories: (1) Direct tax reduction for 180 types of American goods; (2) From now on, American goods will be subject to the lowest tax rate paid by any non-British Empire country; (3) Canada may not freely assess the value of American goods when taxing them; (4) Canadian merchants and travelers returning from the United States will be allowed to bring in duty-free textiles, vegetables, fruits, fish, agricultural and industrial machinery, automobiles, steel, iron, groceries, electrical materials, railway materials, rubber goods, gasoline, chemicals, wooden and paper sundries, etc. The United States has also reduced duties on a wide range of Canadian goods, such as livestock, butter, lumber, etc., as well as many types of newspapers, fish products, mineral products, and furs, which can be imported duty-free. The agreement also includes a clause to safeguard free trade between the United States and its territories, and stipulates that even if the political status of the Philippines changes, the United States will still be able to grant it special conveniences. This clause is also included in the recently drafted US-Colombia trade agreement. The US-Canada treaty also recognizes Cuba's preferential status. Japan, due to the most-favored-nation clause in the US-Japan trade agreement, will naturally receive the same treatment as Canada. However, the goods of Japan and Canada do not generally compete in the US market, so this is not of great significance. Furthermore, the United States and Canada have agreed in the treaty that if either country implements exchange controls in the future, it should grant the other party a fair exchange rate. If the exchange rate difference between the two countries becomes too large, either country can propose revising the treaty. The agreement excludes the Philippine Islands, Samoa, and Guam. (National Telegram, 17th)

After the publication of the Ottawa US-Canada Reciprocal Trade Agreement today, there has been a reaction in Canada. It was learned today that after Parliament convenes, Conservative Party members will rise up in opposition. Generally, Conservative Party members say that Canada's concessions to the United States far exceed those of the United States to Canada, and Canada's interests will suffer greatly. However, this opposition movement will inevitably fail because the Liberal Party has a strong force in the Lower House, and Prime Minister King, who negotiated this agreement, is the leader of that party. (National Telegram, 17th)

US Businesses Feel Uneasy About the Removal of Tariff Barriers

(Washington) The rapid conclusion of the US-Canada trade agreement, and the government's disclosure of the strict terms of the agreement, indicate that American manufacturers and merchants are about to launch a strong protest because their tariff protections have now been removed or reduced. The government stated that it will explain to the country that it has little hope for the agreement, so there will be no opportunity to protest. (National Telegram, 17th)

Officials declare that the agreement is quite satisfactory. However, private individuals inevitably express some concerns. Many British people believe that the economic power of the United States has now deeply penetrated Canada, and Canada's affiliation with Britain will inevitably lose its meaning one day. Some British exporters and industrialists are deeply concerned about the impact of the new agreement on the Ottawa Imperial Trade Agreement. (National Telegram, 17th)

To Resolve Old Debts: British-Russian Negotiations in Progress; Progress in Financial Relations Between the Two Countries 31

(London) The price of old Russian imperial bonds rose by more than 2% today, as rumors of negotiations making Soviet Russia recognize the bonds resurfaced. It is widely expected that the method proposed by Conservative Party member Sir Robert Horne may be a compromise to resolve the Russian debt issue. According to this method, Soviet Russia could raise loans in London with a treasury guarantee at an annual interest rate of 6-7%, and those who subscribe to these loans would only receive an annual interest rate of 3%, with the remaining interest used to clear old Russian pre-war debts. As for the funds raised, most of them would be used to purchase British goods, such as railway materials. According to Reuters, negotiations are currently underway to extend the existing credit facility to Russia when the bond matures in March next year. This shows that there has been progress in financial relations between Britain and Russia. (Reuters Dispatch, 18th)

Ministry of Finance Explains Foreign Exchange and Commodity Price Questions 34

(Nanjing) After the implementation of the new currency policy, the general public has doubts about whether foreign exchange and commodity prices can be stabilized, whether legal currency can be widely circulated, and whether reserves are adequate. The Ministry of Finance now explains as follows: (1) Foreign exchange stability issue: The three banks' unrestricted foreign exchange trading already has the function of regulating and controlling supply and demand. There is no problem with exchange rate stability. Since the implementation of the new system, the foreign exchange rates quoted by the central bank and foreign banks have not changed much. Compared with before the implementation, the exchange rate has not differed much. Foreign exchange is indeed trending towards stability, and the steps of various foreign banks can be consistent; (2) Commodity price stability issue: The commodity price increase at the beginning of the implementation of the new system was a temporary stimulus because of the misunderstanding that the new system was currency inflation. Now that the truth has been clarified, commodity prices are gradually falling. However, after a considerable period of time, due to the improvement of the issuance system and financial system, social currency has reasonable circulation, funds and credit have reasonable use, and foreign exchange is stable, international trade will fully develop, and commodity prices will naturally have a gradual upward trend. However, this is the result of national economic prosperity; (3) Universal circulation issue: Some say that Chinese people are accustomed to having silver coins and suddenly using legal currency, fearing that it cannot be widely circulated. In fact, in recent years, bank notes have already been circulating in the inland areas, which has cultivated people's habit of using banknotes, and the cash reserve ratio of our country's legal currency is higher than that of any other country, with solid credit, and universal circulation is not a problem; (4) Reserve adequacy issue: There is a misunderstanding that the cash reserves of various banks are empty, so the new system is promulgated to restrict it, and only legal currency can be used domestically. In fact, the issuance reserves of various banks are quite substantial. The current reserve ratio is above 60%. The issuance of legal currency is even more based on reserves as a representative, so the issuance reserves of legal currency will be more adequate in the future, and there is no problem. (Central News Agency Telegram, 18th)

(Nanjing) A spokesman for the Ministry of Finance said that countries around the world, in view of the seriousness of financial and monetary issues, are all adopting self-defense policies. The methods are roughly as follows: England suspended the gold standard in 1931; the United States suspended the gold standard in 1933 and implemented foreign exchange control; Germany implemented foreign exchange control in 1931 and exempted from cash redemption obligations; Japan suspended the gold standard in 1931 and foreign exchange control in 1932; Italy implemented foreign exchange control in 1934; Austria implemented foreign exchange control in 1931 and suspended the gold standard in 1933; Argentina suspended the gold standard in 1929 and implemented foreign exchange control in 1931; Brazil implemented foreign exchange control in 1931; Canada, Finland, Mexico, and Norway all suspended the gold standard in 1931; Siam suspended the gold standard in 1932; the Czech Republic implemented foreign exchange control in 1931 and suspended the gold standard in 1934; Turkey implemented foreign exchange control in 1930. Our country has always been on the silver standard, which is unfavorable when exchanging currencies with gold standard countries, and the outflow of silver in recent years has greatly threatened the economic foundation. In view of this crisis, the Ministry of Finance had no choice but to decide to implement a monetary system that stabilizes finance and revives the economy. (Central News Agency Telegram, 18th)

(Hong Kong) Foreign exchange has been slightly stabilized in recent days, and the business community is showing improvement compared to before. The provincial government is advising foreign banks in Shamian to exchange their silver reserves for legal currency from provincial banks. (Central News Agency Telegram, 18th)

The original text is very long, and the outline is as follows: (1) The need for a monetary policy; (2) The key points of the new monetary system; (3) The essence of the new monetary system; (4) The new monetary system is by no means abandoning the silver standard; (5) The new monetary system is by no means currency inflation; (6) To those who doubt the new monetary system; (7) Benefits of implementing the new monetary system. In addition, the important orders for the implementation of legal currency are attached as a compilation for reference. (Central News Agency Telegram, 18th)

Shen Baixian Discusses Yellow River Flood Control Work 57

(Zhenjiang) Director of the Jiangsu Department of Construction Shen Baixian discussed the Yellow River flood control work in Jiangsu Province since April. The principle is to control and divert simultaneously. A total of eleven counties, including Tongshan, Pei, Pi, Feng, Huai, and Su, participated in the work, constructing 940 kilometers of levees with 11,895,000 cubic meters of earthwork, mobilizing 1,060,000 laborers. However, the Yellow River flow exceeded the controlled diversion capacity, resulting in disasters in ten counties, including Tongshan, Pei, Pi, Feng, Su, Si, Lian, Shu, and Huaidong, with an area of approximately 8,800,000 mu and losses exceeding 100 million yuan. Although the water level has stabilized somewhat, the breaches have not been closed, and the main flow remains strong, with 80% of the total flow. The downstream flow still exceeds the specified standard, remaining dangerous. Therefore, in addition to hoping for early closure of the breaches, the most important tasks are post-disaster reconstruction and relief work. Furthermore, Jiangsu Province is expediting the completion of the Huai River diversion project into the sea by April next year in preparation for potential simultaneous flooding of the Yellow and Huai Rivers. (18th Central News Agency dispatch)

Tianjin-Baoding Highway Construction Begins 59

(Baoding) Construction of the Tianjin-Baoding Highway commenced on the 18th. Labor is being conscripted in four sections, with 3,000 people per section, supervised by the construction departments of each county in conjunction with the Tianjin-Baoding Highway Engineering Office. It is a misunderstanding that the establishment of the Philippine government has resulted in overseas Filipino residents in Xiamen losing their U.S. citizenship and being unable to enjoy consular jurisdiction. Fuzhou: Southeastern Bank Suspends Operations; Tianji Money Shop Also Runs Aground 75

Fuzhou Correspondence: Since the adoption of the legal tender in this city, the financial situation has been relatively stable. Although prices once rose, they gradually fell afterwards. The public is quite optimistic about the future of the new monetary policy. However, from the 13th, the Southeastern Bank and Tianji Money Shop suddenly ran aground one after another. The Farmers' Bank, Xintai Bank, and other money shops such as Xiangkang, Jiuhe, and Zijue all experienced bank runs, creating a huge financial turmoil. The Southeastern Bank was established in the 18th year of the Republic and was jointly operated by naval circles and baojuan (tax farmers). It has a capital of 300,000 yuan and issues banknotes in denominations of ten yuan, five yuan, and one yuan. The military's payroll and tax payments mostly use it. Over the years, business has been relatively developed. The banknotes in circulation in northeastern Fujian are about 600,000 yuan, and those used in this city are about 300,000 yuan. The bank also manages real estate trading, and most of its loans are based on credit. The value of real estate pledged is more than 600,000 yuan, and credit loans are more than 300,000 yuan. Recently, due to the government's implementation of legal tender, there have been rumors in the market that the bank is unstable. Banknotes circulating in northeastern Fujian have gradually returned to Fuzhou, and many people have been cashing them out. On the 13th, the bank's cash reserves were only 60,000 yuan. It attempted to pledge real estate deeds to borrow 240,000 yuan from the banking community for turnover, but the banks were all tight on cash and could not reach an agreement. The bank had no choice but to cease operations temporarily and asked the Provincial Bank to dispatch a manager and two assistants to the bank to check the accounts. The market was greatly shocked to see the bank suddenly cease operations, and rumors arose. China Farmers' Bank and Shanghai Xintai Bank, both branches, were affected. Bank runs occurred on the afternoon of the 14th. Fortunately, both banks were able to cope adequately, and the turmoil subsided by evening. On the morning of the 15th, the Tianji, Xiangkang, Jiuhe, and Zifeng money shops also experienced bank runs. The Tianji Money Shop was unable to cope. The owner of the shop, Lin Qigui, and the manager, Zhou Peiqin, went to the Public Security Bureau to surrender and requested a seal. The shop had issued 110,000 yuan in tickets, and had 40,000 yuan in external deposits, while the recoverable accounts and real estate were valued at only 500,000 yuan, a huge difference. The other three money shops each paid out 20,000 to 50,000 yuan before the turmoil subsided. On the afternoon of the 15th, the Southeastern Bank held a temporary directors' meeting to discuss liquidation measures. However, the difference between the assets and cash reserves was too large, and the loans issued could not be immediately recovered, so no solution was reached. The bank's directors, Yang Shoutu, Yao Fuqian, Chen Jianjun, and Deputy Manager Chen Buyi are all being monitored within the head office. Since the turmoil began, market prices have increased again, and shops arbitrarily refuse to use banknotes from banks and money shops, and people's hearts are quite restless. The Provincial Government issued a proclamation prohibiting villains from spreading rumors and disrupting finance, and violators will be punished according to the Emergency Punishment Law. The Chamber of Commerce also held an emergency meeting on the evening of the 15th and resolved to telegraph the Ministry of Finance to order the Central Bank to allocate 1 million yuan to supply merchants, with real estate mortgaged to obtain cash to maintain commerce, but it is unknown whether this will be approved. (November 16)

Wuxi: Five Silk Factories Suspend Production Due to Lack of Raw Materials 77

Since the summer and autumn of this year, silk prices have been rising, and silk sales have been smooth. Silk merchants in Wuxi have been planning to open factories, and there are already 31, which has led to the vision of a silk factory industry revival. However, due to the lack of raw materials and high cocoon prices, various factories are forced to suspend production. Yesterday, it was learned that five silk factories, including Huigongqiao Baisi, Zhanghuangmiao Xinchang, Nanqiao Yichang, Lihuazhuang Wanchang, and Yonghua, have already suspended production one after another. Recently, the market price of dry cocoons is 220 yuan per dan, but because the monetary situation is extremely tight, there are few transactions.

Strict Prohibition of Women's Permed Hair 78

The County Government held an administrative meeting at 10:00 AM yesterday (the 18th), chaired by Section Chief Shao, and resolved: (1) The white sheds along the city wall near Jixiang Bridge are obstructing road administration and must be demolished. (2) The sewers on the streets of Shenguo Lane and Nanmen Cotton Lane, and the areas along the Yingshan River at the bottom of the Huayuan Lane, are severely damaged and will be repaired by the county allocating funds. (3) A private prostitute shelter will be established. (4) Women's permed hair goes against the simple and unadorned spirit of the new life movement. The county will order the Education Bureau to instruct the principals of various schools to advise staff and students not to perm their hair as a model for society. Those who do not follow the advice will have their teachers and staff resign and students expelled. At the same time, the Public Security Bureau will be ordered to strictly prohibit all barbershops from offering perms, and violators will be punished.

An unidentified female corpse, approximately 50 years old, was discovered in the Dongyaogou area of Xinzha Town in the Second District of Wujin County. The local village head, Yu Yulin, reported it to the local court. Chief Prosecutor Yang Kongxi personally went to investigate on the 17th. It was found that the corpse had contusions on her throat and back. She was murdered before death. It was discovered that there was a kerosene box under the head of the corpse. Upon inspection, it contained the spirit tablet of the deceased's late husband, Peng Xifu. There were also some scattered objects beside her. It was discovered that the deceased had a son named Xiaozhen, whose whereabouts are unknown. Chief Prosecutor Yang believes that the case is complicated and the truth is unclear, and ordered the local village head and others to strictly investigate and arrest the murderer and bring him to justice.

Education Broadcasting Special Edition

The Process of Implementing Educational Broadcasting 84

— Xu Yiqiao, Section Chief of the Ministry of Education

1. Today's educational broadcast program is about "The Process of Implementing Educational Broadcasting by the Ministry of Education." Since the Ministry began educational broadcasting on Double Tenth Day, we have broadcast more than twenty times, but we haven't talked about the meaning and process of the Ministry's implementation of educational broadcasting. Therefore, we think it is necessary to have a chance to talk to everyone.

2. Educational broadcasting is a new educational tool that emerged after the European War. In short, its meaning is to use radio waves to transmit knowledge about education. This new educational tool can be said to be a major revolution in the method of transmitting knowledge since the invention of printing. Because it takes a long time for knowledge to be transmitted through printed matter, and the effect is slow, and the printed matter itself is not easily obtained by the general public. As for educational broadcasting, it is tantamount to using the radio as a general lecture platform, and using places equipped with radios as lecture seats. Each radio can have hundreds of people listening, or thousands or even tens of thousands of people listening. Now that radios are becoming cheaper, people can buy a radio at a small cost to enable countless people to receive the latest knowledge broadcast by the radio. The impact on education is naturally easy to imagine. Therefore, this new tool of educational broadcasting is a major revolution in the method of transmitting knowledge since the invention of printing.

The use of radio waves to broadcast educational knowledge in European and American countries can be traced back to the Chelmeford Station of Marchoni Company in the UK in 1920. Since then, countries have followed suit and become increasingly developed, and the plans have become increasingly systematic and organized. Now, so-called broadcasting education has become the most important new educational tool in various countries. As for broadcasting stations in our country, there has certainly been no shortage of educational broadcasting programs in the past, but compared with European and American countries, the degree of utilization is naturally still very different.

3. This time, the Ministry implemented educational broadcasting. On the one hand, it was because it recognized the immaturity of public knowledge and believed that it was necessary to use this new tool to give them sufficient new knowledge. On the other hand, because domestic broadcasting stations in the past were limited by the design of other programs, they had not been able to systematically broadcast knowledge in the field of education. Therefore, in May of this year, we discussed with the Central Party Headquarters how to use the Central Broadcasting Station to further promote this new educational tool. This is the beginning of the Ministry's implementation of educational broadcasting.

In May of this year, the Ministry decided to start educational broadcasting for students in secondary schools and the general public across the country. Therefore, we formulated and promulgated the General Outline for the Installation of Radio Receivers in Secondary Schools and Public Education Halls Across the Country, ordering secondary schools and public education halls that have not installed radio receivers to complete the installation in three semesters starting from the 24th year [of the Republic], and submit plans to the Ministry in stages by the relevant competent educational administrative authorities. At the same time, the Ministry pre-ordered 1,000 radio receivers from the Construction Committee, including AC machines, storage battery machines, and dry battery machines, based on the phased plans pre-ordered by the education departments and bureaus of various provinces and cities, and distributed them in batches for installation. The above-mentioned installation schedules have been largely submitted to the Ministry by the education departments and bureaus of various provinces and cities. Some places that have not submitted or have not submitted completely will be able to submit them completely in the shortest possible time after being urged by the Ministry.

Next, I want to talk about the Ministry's training of radio instructors. The Ministry, recognizing the lack of radio technicians in secondary schools and public education halls in various provinces and cities, believed that it was necessary to open a special class for training. Therefore, from July 20 to August 20 of this year, we held a National Training Class for Radio Instructors in Secondary Schools and Public Education Halls. The students were selected by the education departments and bureaus from their own staff. Although this training class lasted only one month, because it focused on radio practice and the teachers were all technicians with practical experience from the Central Broadcasting Station, the graduates were able to understand and apply the installation, repair, and reception methods of radios. Now they have all graduated and returned to their original dispatch agencies to serve. Their task is to guide the installation, repair, and reception methods of radios in various secondary schools and public education halls, and they have a major task in promoting educational broadcasting.

The third point to mention is the Ministry's method of hiring educational broadcasters. The Ministry, recognizing the importance of educational broadcasting, hired lecturers who are all experts with a great deal of experience in the topics they are lecturing on or the responsible personnel of government agencies. At the same time, in order to systematize the teaching materials, we also had thorough discussions in advance on how to enable secondary school students and the general public to obtain the latest and most needed knowledge. In order to make everyone clear about the content of the lectures, the items and times of each semester's broadcasts are listed below:

The items mentioned above for secondary school students and the general public are broadcast daily. Every Tuesday, Thursday, and Saturday, from 4:30 PM to 5:00 PM, they are broadcast for secondary school students. Every Monday, Wednesday, Friday, and Sunday afternoon, from 6:30 PM to 7:00 PM, they are broadcast for the general public. As for the detailed topics of each item, they have also been planned and prepared in advance, and a list of programs has been distributed to all secondary schools and public education halls across the country, so there is no need to elaborate on them here.

Finally, one more point is that the Ministry implements broadcasting education with the purpose of enabling secondary school students and the general public to obtain practical supplementary knowledge. Therefore, detailed methods have been formulated on how to use broadcasting education so that various secondary schools and public education halls have a basis for their work. These methods, which have now been promulgated, include two types: Guidelines for the Use of Broadcasting Education in Secondary Schools and Guidelines for the Use of Broadcasting Education in Public Education Halls. Among them, regarding secondary schools, the school authorities must make students understand the time, topic, and lecturer of each broadcast in advance. Each time a broadcast is made, all students must be gathered to listen and take notes. After the lecture, the teacher must add a summary explanation. During examinations, questions related to the content of the broadcast must be inserted. At the same time, when educational administrative authorities inspect various schools, the use of broadcasting education should also be used as one of the strict assessment tasks. Regarding public education halls, the director of the hall must quickly contact local enthusiastic educators to share the responsibility of enabling the public to use educational broadcasting, and make sure that the public can come to listen on time, summarize and explain after listening, and post in appropriate places so that the public can obtain the practical benefits of educational broadcasting.

The above is a general overview of the meaning and process of the Ministry's implementation of educational broadcasting. Because educational broadcasting has only recently begun, I am afraid that everyone still cannot fully understand the past process and the meaning of implementation. Therefore, today I specifically used this time to make a general report. I hope that all educational administrative authorities, schools, public education halls, and other social education institutions across the country will pay attention to this issue and share the responsibility of promotion. (End)

Local News

City Land Bureau Establishes Land Consolidation Committee to Publicly Study Land Consolidation Issues 85

Since Cai Zengji took office as Director of the Municipal Land Bureau, land administration matters have greatly improved, and previously unresolved pending cases have also been gradually cleared. It is learned that in order to further publicly study various issues related to land consolidation in the city, Cai has specially organized a land committee in the bureau to jointly promote its progress. In addition to the Director serving as the chairman of the committee and the heads of each department as ex-officio members, many experts with rich land administration experience and legal technical expertise have also been invited to serve as members of the committee. It was established on the 15th, and the first meeting was held, passing the articles of association. The articles of association and minutes are recorded as follows:

Articles of Association

Article of Association of the Land Consolidation Committee (Article 1): The bureau has established a Land Consolidation Committee for the purpose of consolidating land and improving various systems for surveying, issuing new certificates, registering, and recording. (Article 2): The committee shall have one chairman and a number of members, organized by the following personnel: (1) The Director of the bureau shall be the chairman of the committee. (2) The heads of each department of the bureau shall be ex-officio members of the committee. (3) The Director of the bureau shall appoint a number of experts as members. (Article 3): The committee shall deliberate on the following matters: (1) Matters concerning the reform of the surveying system. (2) Matters concerning the improvement of the certificate renewal and registration system. (3) Planning and designing land registration. (4) Matters concerning improving administrative efficiency. (5) All matters concerning land consolidation. (6) Matters concerning the determination of land prices in areas where land value tax has not been implemented. (Article 5): The committee shall meet once every two weeks to resolve matters listed in the preceding article, which shall be submitted by the chairman for discussion or proposed by the members. (Article 6): The committee meeting shall synthesize the opinions of the members, and the chairman shall make a decision after deliberation. (Article 7): The committee shall submit the resolutions of each case in accordance with the provisions of the preceding article to the relevant departments of the Land Bureau for implementation. (Article 8): The bureau chief shall appoint staff members to handle the整理編製 of meeting records and meeting documents of the committee. (Article 9): These articles shall be implemented upon approval by the Director of the bureau.

First Meeting

The Municipal Land Bureau Land Consolidation Committee was established on the 15th and held its first meeting. Chairman: Director Cai Zengji. (A) Report Matters: (1) Chairman's Report: The land situation in the city is complex and requires consolidation. We have established this committee to jointly promote progress. You gentlemen are either practically responsible for the administration of the Land Bureau, or rich in land administration experience, or legal technical experts. I deeply believe that the city's land problems can be simplified with your assistance, and everything can be solved easily. The important matters that the committee should study and carry out at present are as follows: (1) Clearing up the Land Bureau's pending cases. (2) Improving the Land Bureau's existing system. (3) Implementing land registration. (4) Determining the valuation standards for land that has not been subject to land value tax. In addition, there are also problems such as thoroughly investigating the addresses of land value tax payers that are unknown, compiling annual rent collection registers, considering tax increases, and charging the people in installments. These issues also need to be studied separately. I hope that all members will express their opinions to gather wisdom from all sources. (2) Member Fan Yongzeng reported that land surveying in the city began in 1924, handled by the local Land Surveying Bureau. Its purpose was to clarify boundaries and correct grain quotas. In 1927, the Land Bureau was established and handled land surveying business. First, it re-measured triangles, supplemented survey guide lines, and implemented plane surveying. In more prosperous areas, theodolite surveying was used. After the survey was completed, drawings were made, and certificates were exchanged within a limited time based on the scope of the old drawings. At present, 70% of the old Shanghai County has been surveyed, and 50% have been announced for certificate exchange. More than 100,000 land certificates have been issued. (3) Member Zhu Zhaohuang reported that the Land Bureau's fourth department has many pending cases, the reasons for which are: (1) People have not submitted evidence. (2) Court lawsuits have not been completed. (3) Surveying and mapping procedures have not been completed. Regarding the first point, staff members have been assigned to specifically organize and urge the conclusion of the first point. The second point can only be handled after the court case is concluded. Regarding the third point, the third department is expediting it. In addition, thousands of land certificates have been completed after days of expediting the filling of forms. Member Lu Dachi reported that the Land Bureau's second department's pending cases are mostly due to incomplete evidence or owners leaving Shanghai, so they cannot be processed. (B) Discussion Matters: (1) The committee's articles of association were passed. (2) The committee's subgroup list was passed. (3) Request that the Land Bureau's competent departments provide written explanations of all business handling procedures, along with current regulations, and send them to the members to clarify the actual situation and facilitate deliberation. Resolution: The current regulations shall be printed within four days, and the procedures shall be clarified and completed within one week. Both shall be submitted to the committee's recorder for distribution. (4) The first subgroup meeting will be held. Resolution: A. The first subgroup meeting dates are as follows: Legal Regulations Group, 2:00 PM on the 19th of this month (Tuesday); Administrative Group, 10:00 AM on the 21st of this month (Thursday); Technical Group, 2:00 PM on the 23rd of this month (Saturday). B. The subgroup meeting records shall be handled by the convening member of each group, who shall appoint Land Bureau staff members to handle it.

China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's New Haiyuan Ship Run Aground in Guangdong, Now Planning to Transfer Passengers and Unload Cargo to Lighten Load and Escape Danger 86

China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's new Haiyuan ship ran aground in Guangdong yesterday, according to a telegram. It is currently transferring cargo to be rescued. The details are being investigated as follows:

Reasons for Running Aground

The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's Haiyuan ship is the first of the new Sihai ships built with Gengkuan funds. The ship's price is 1.4 million yuan. The ship operates on the Shanghai-Shantou-Guangdong line and is the official passenger ship of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's Nanhua fleet. It travels back and forth on a fixed schedule without any delay. This time, it went from Shanghai to Guangdong, first to Shantou and Hong Kong to unload cargo and passengers, and then to Guangzhou. At 5:00 AM on the 17th of this month, the ship sailed to Taishik Borreer in Huangpu, Guangdong. At that time, heavy fog occurred on the harbor. The Haiyuan ship planned to go to Bai'etan, but was blocked by the fog and mistakenly entered the channel, causing it to run aground on the shoal, and the hull sank into the shallow sand and mud.

Escape Awaits

After the Haiyuan ship ran aground, the captain, Strong Hannason, first applied full power to try to escape danger by himself in the harbor. However, the ship was still heavily loaded, the ship's draft was quite deep, and the tide was low, so it was really difficult. The captain had no choice but to send a telegram to Shanghai to report. It was Sunday, and business was suspended, so yesterday morning, an urgent telegram was sent to the Guangdong branch to be rescued as soon as possible.

Transfer and Towing

It is learned that the head office urgently telegraphed the Guangdong branch yesterday, roughly ordering the Guangdong branch to quickly send barges to the grounding site, Taishik Borreer, first to find a way to transfer the passengers on the Haiyuan ship to Bai'etan to disembark, so as to avoid passengers' anxiety, and then order a part of the heavy cargo on the ship to be transferred in order to reduce the load and float on the harbor surface at high tide, and then carry out towing rescue to Guangzhou. According to the person in charge of the bureau, the place where the Haiyuan ship ran aground is near Bai'etan in Guangdong. Once the goods are transferred, it is expected to be towed out. However, the head office withheld the news until last night, so the insurance company has been notified. It is noted that the ship was originally scheduled to arrive in Shanghai on the 21st. Now that it has run aground, it is difficult to predict whether it will arrive on schedule.

Business Handling of Various Banks and Firms: Cash Handling Measures, Ministry of Finance Instructs the Silver and Money Industry Association to Handle in Accordance with the Original Certificate领劵 Method 87

The Ministry of Finance instructed the Shanghai Silver and Money Industry Association yesterday, saying that since the implementation of the legal currency, all cash prepared by various issuing banks and cash used for business purposes by various silver and money industries have been sealed and stored in accordance with the ministry's order. In order to revitalize the market, in addition to the cash prepared for issuance, which should be fully handed over to the Central Bank of China, the cash that has been sealed for business purposes and the cash received from the exchange of legal currency shall be allowed to be exchanged for legal currency by each bank and firm at a rate of 60% cash plus 40% government bonds to the Central Bank of China or use legal currency in accordance with the regulations. Those who use legal currency shall still sign a certificate领劵 contract to comply with it. In addition to informing the Central Bank, it is hereby ordered that you be informed and that all colleagues be notified accordingly.

Latvian Nationals Held the 17th Anniversary Yesterday 92

Yesterday was the 17th anniversary of the independence of the Republic of Latvia. Latvian nationals in this port held a celebration, which was very exciting. Latvia is located on the shores of the Baltic Sea, 陀迦伐 A major transportation hub in Europe, and in ancient times, it was repeatedly at war with the Danes, Russians, Swedes, and Poles, becoming a famous battlefield. By the 18th century, it was completely destroyed and incorporated into the Russian territory. After the end of the European War, it gained independence. This was the first time in seven hundred years that its people had regained their freedom. Most of the people live by animal husbandry, farming, fishing, and hunting. After the country was destroyed, many of its people fled to various places, so there is probably no major city in the world today that does not have Latvians. There are currently 300 people living in Shanghai, most of whom are refugees from the European War. There are now about 2 million people in the country, who are of Indo-European descent. Their language still preserves ancient forms, which is a must-learn for researchers of philosophy. The level of education in the country is very high. The government spends about 20 million yuan in Shanghai currency on education each year. The University of Latvia has 11 subjects and about 7,000 students. English is a compulsory subject and Wibble also studies it. In 1933, there were 153 daily newspapers, 250 weekly and monthly magazines in the country. The current president is Mr. Korisis, and his prime minister and foreign minister, Mr. Upomanis, is highly respected by the people and is called "Uncle."

Telegram Political Bonds Mortgage Loan: Contract Signing Begins 93

Total Amount of 6 Million Yuan, Each Bank Borrows Separately. Interest Rate of 8%, Repaid in One Year, Payment to Be Made Soon.

The Ministry of Communications' telegram political bonds of 10 million yuan contacted the Shanghai banking community to mortgage 6 million yuan in cash. The total amount is 6 million yuan. The amount borrowed by each bank is as follows: Central Bank, Bank of China, and Bank of Communications jointly recognized 3.1 million yuan, Postal Savings and Remittance Bureau 1.2 million yuan, Shanghai Bank 200,000 yuan, Jincheng Bank and Zhongnan Bank 250,000 yuan each, Salt Bank and Mainland Bank 200,000 yuan each, Zhejiang Industrial Bank and Industrial Bank 150,000 yuan each, Guohuo Bank and Siming Bank 100,000 yuan each, and Kenye Bank and Guohua Bank 50,000 yuan each. The total is 6 million yuan. It is expected to be repaid in one year with an interest rate of 8%. International electricity fee income is used as a guarantee. Zhou Wenduan, the director of the Telegraph Administration Department of the Ministry of Communications, who is a representative of the Ministry of Communications, has begun to sign the loan agreement signed by Zhu Jiahua, the Minister of Communications, with the lending banks separately. Silk Promotion Committee Announces the Number of Dried Cocoons in Jiangsu and Zhejiang Provinces: Export Value of 18 Million Yuan This Year, Planned to Manufacture 2.5 Million Silkworm Eggs Next Spring 94

Silk factories in Shanghai will suspend all operations due to the sharp increase in exports and the shortage of raw materials. The industry association attributes this to the influence of Zhejiang Province's control of raw silk. The reporter of 華東 News Agency inquired about this from the Shanghai office of the Zhejiang Provincial Raw Silk Promotion Committee. The person in charge of the office announced the details as follows:

190,000担 of Cocoons Collected This Year

According to the survey reports of the Silk Improvement Association in spring and autumn this year, the amount of cocoons collected in Jiangsu and Zhejiang is a total of 181,000 担 (Dry cocoons) measured by 司马秤, plus 17,000 担 of previous stocks of new cocoons, totaling 198,000 担, which can produce 45,000 担 of raw silk.

Raw Silk Exports Exceed 10 Million

From June to the end of October, according to the report of the Commodity Inspection Bureau, a total of 22,903 担 of white factory silk were exported, an average of about 4,600 担 per month. The value of raw silk exported this year is about 18,400,000, and silk factories have earned more than 4 million yuan.

110,000 担 of Cocoons Currently in Stock

At the end of October, according to the survey report of the Silk Improvement Association, there were a total of 112,269 担 of dried cocoons in stock in Jiangsu and Zhejiang, which can produce 24,900 祖 of raw silk. According to the export volume in the previous five months, it can last until the end of March next year. Since the start of work this summer, 87 silk factories in Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces with 23,197 silk reeling machines have reeled only 76,000 祖 of dried cocoons.

Government Work Should Stop Appropriately

The increase in silk prices this year and the increase in the number of factories starting work have resulted in the failure to receive new raw materials. If the silk prices go the other way, there will be a surplus of raw materials, which is completely unrelated to the Zhejiang Province's control. As for the Zhejiang Provincial Construction Department's collection of cocoons, it started in the autumn of 1934. At that time, because no one cared about silk cocoons and it was also a year of severe drought, the government came out to buy them to maintain the lives of farmers. As for those purchased by the Construction Department this year, only 20% of the province's silk cocoons were purchased, and the cocoons collected were all reeled by silk factories with better equipment and work in Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and Shanghai. There was no distinction between provincial boundaries from the beginning. If the silk market can continue to maintain its current price, farmers and manufacturers can live and work in peace next year. Government work can be limited to increasing the manufacture of silkworm eggs, guiding farmers in silkworm breeding, improving silk reeling technology, and uniformly promoting raw silk. As for the work of the promotion office this year, a uniform brand is used to promote sales in Europe and the United States. Since its opening, the selling price has changed from low to high, all following the market, and it has never been raised or suppressed, so that the raw silk trade can be circulated. It is also a trivial matter to deliver goods on schedule and ensure the quality. Shanghai exporters are very satisfied with the control measures and promotion work. They all say that if the promotion of Chinese silk can be unified and credit is emphasized, foreign trade can develop faster. In short, the government's overall planning for the control of raw silk is based on the overall situation. It is hoped that the silk factory industry can also pool their efforts and cooperate with each other, and the future of the silk industry will have a brighter future.

Increase Silkworm Egg Production Next Spring

Also, according to the Shanghai office of the Silk Improvement Committee, the National Economic Commission has planned to expand the scope and increase the manufacture of silkworm eggs during the spring silkworm season next year. There are currently 2 million improved species, and another 500,000 will be purchased to be distributed to various provinces for application during the spring silkworm breeding season. It is learned that farmers in various silkworm areas have great faith in improved varieties. Since the late autumn silkworms entered the market, they have registered with the guidance offices. In addition to setting up model silkworm leaf improvement farms in various provinces, the work of cultivating mulberry trees in various regions is also being carried out in cooperation with the China Silkworm Improvement Committee.

The 150th Anniversary of Sino-US Commerce to be Grandly Celebrated Tonight 97

The celebration commemorating the 150th anniversary of Sino-US commerce is scheduled to be held tonight at 8:00 PM at the American Club on Fuzhou Road. The ceremony will be quite grand, with over two hundred invitations having been sent out. A Central News Agency reporter interviewed Mr.賀, the secretary of the American Chamber of Commerce, yesterday, who provided the following details:

Recalling the Past

Sino-US trade, from its inception to the present, spans one hundred and fifty years. On this day in 1825, the American merchant ship "Empress of China" returned to New York from Guangzhou, taking six months. At that time, Britain was engaged in development in Africa, so Sino-US trade gradually developed from then on. Coupled with scientific advancements and rapid progress in various industries, celebrations are held annually on this day, partly to promote the development of trade between China and the United States, and partly to foster Sino-US diplomatic relations.

Tonight's Celebration

Tonight's celebration will be on a grand scale. Prominent figures from both China and the United States, such as 孔祥熙, 孫哲生, 宋子文, 蔡元培, 吳鐵城, 顧維鈞, and representatives from various circles in this city, are all among the invited guests, totaling over two hundred people. Various recreational activities will be held in the evening to entertain the guests.

The Jiangsu Second Prison in Caohejing, Shanghai, is a model prison with the most perfect facilities. It is large in scale, holding over three thousand prisoners. Additional 100,000 Still Lacking; Decided to Use Surplus from Spring Cocoons

The World News Agency reports that the Sericulture Control Committee of the Construction Department of Zhejiang Province, in view of the booming overseas sales of Chinese silk and the increasing silk prices since the outbreak of the European Italian-Ethiopian War, intends to fundamentally improve Chinese silk products in order to enhance international trade and establish the reputation of Chinese silk. It is estimated that silkworm farmers throughout the province will need about 1.2 million sheets of improved spring silkworm eggs during the spring silkworm season next year. For advance preparation, special commissioners have been dispatched to silkworm egg production farms in Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces to order one million sheets of improved eggs. The required funding for ordering eggs is estimated to be 300,000 yuan. Due to the province's financial constraints, it is difficult to allocate funds. The committee is contacting various banks, including the China Communications Bank, to negotiate loans for ordering eggs. According to banking circles, after several rounds of negotiations, the China and Communications Banks have agreed to lend 100,000 yuan each, using the spring silkworm eggs as collateral, with an annual interest rate of 1% and repayment of principal and interest within six months. A formal contract will be signed and payment will be made soon. The remaining 100,000 yuan will be used from the 100,000 yuan surplus from this year's spring cocoons by the Sericulture Control Committee.
